    *   [Agents](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#agents)
    
*   [Evaluations and Comparisons](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#evaluations-and-comparisons)
    
    *   [LLaVa-13, Fuyu-8B, and MiniGPT-4 Multi-Modal LLM Models Comparison for Image Reasoning](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#llava-13-fuyu-8b-and-minigpt-4-multi-modal-llm-models-comparison-for-image-reasoning)
    *   [Simple Evaluation of Multi-Modal RAG](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#simple-evaluation-of-multi-modal-rag)
    
*   [Model Guides](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#model-guides)

Multi-modal[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#multi-modal "Permanent link")
=======================================================================================================

LlamaIndex offers capabilities to not only build language-based applications but also **multi-modal** applications - combining language and images.

Types of Multi-modal Use Cases[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#types-of-multi-modal-use-cases "Permanent link")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This space is actively being explored right now, but some fascinating use cases are popping up.

### RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation)[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#rag-retrieval-augmented-generation "Permanent link")

All the core RAG concepts: indexing, retrieval, and synthesis, can be extended into the image setting.

*   The input could be text or image.
*   The stored knowledge base can consist of text or images.
*   The inputs to response generation can be text or image.
*   The final response can be text or image.

Check out our guides below:

*   [GPT-4V Multi Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/gpt4v_multi_modal_retrieval/)
*   [Multi-modal retrieval with CLIP](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/multi_modal_retrieval/)
*   [Image to Image Retrieval](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/image_to_image_retrieval/)
*   [Structured Image Retrieval](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/structured_image_retrieval/)
*   [Chroma Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/ChromaMultiModalDemo/)
*   [Gemini Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/gemini/)
*   [Ollama Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/ollama_cookbook/)

### Structured Outputs[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#structured-outputs "Permanent link")

You can generate a `structured` output with the new OpenAI GPT4V via LlamaIndex. The user just needs to specify a Pydantic object to define the structure of the output.

Check out the guide below:

*   [Multi-Modal Pydantic Program](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/multi_modal_pydantic/)

### Retrieval-Augmented Image Captioning[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#retrieval-augmented-image-captioning "Permanent link")

Oftentimes understanding an image requires looking up information from a knowledge base. A flow here is retrieval-augmented image captioning - first caption the image with a multi-modal model, then refine the caption by retrieving it from a text corpus.

Check out our guides below:

*   [Llava + Testla 10Q](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/llava_multi_modal_tesla_10q/)

### Agents[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#agents "Permanent link")

Here are some initial works demonstrating agentic capabilities with GPT-4V.

*   [Multi-Modal Agents](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/mm_agent/)
*   [GPT-4V Experiments](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/gpt4v_experiments_cot/)

Evaluations and Comparisons[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#evaluations-and-comparisons "Permanent link")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These sections show comparisons between different multi-modal models for different use cases.

### LLaVa-13, Fuyu-8B, and MiniGPT-4 Multi-Modal LLM Models Comparison for Image Reasoning[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#llava-13-fuyu-8b-and-minigpt-4-multi-modal-llm-models-comparison-for-image-reasoning "Permanent link")

These notebooks show how to use different Multi-Modal LLM models for image understanding/reasoning. The various model inferences are supported by Replicate or OpenAI GPT4-V API. We compared several popular Multi-Modal LLMs:

*   GPT4-V (OpenAI API)
*   LLava-13B (Replicate)
*   Fuyu-8B (Replicate)
*   MiniGPT-4 (Replicate)
*   CogVLM (Replicate)

Check out our guides below:

*   [Replicate Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/replicate_multi_modal/)
*   [GPT4-V](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/openai_multi_modal/)

### Simple Evaluation of Multi-Modal RAG[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#simple-evaluation-of-multi-modal-rag "Permanent link")

In this notebook guide, we'll demonstrate how to evaluate a Multi-Modal RAG system. As in the text-only case, we will consider the evaluation of Retrievers and Generators separately. As we alluded to in our blog on the topic of Evaluating Multi-Modal RAGs, our approach here involves the application of adapted versions of the usual techniques for evaluating both Retriever and Generator (used for the text-only case). These adapted versions are part of the llama-index library (i.e., evaluation module), and this notebook will walk you through how you can apply them to your evaluation use cases.

*   [Multi-Modal RAG Evaluation](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/evaluation/multi_modal/multi_modal_rag_evaluation/)

Model Guides[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#model-guides "Permanent link")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are notebook guides showing you how to interact with different multimodal model providers.

*   [OpenAI Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/openai_multi_modal/)
*   [Replicate Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/replicate_multi_modal/)
*   [Ollama Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/ollama_cookbook/)

Guides](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#model-guides)\n\nMulti-modal[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#multi-modal \"Permanent link\")\n=======================================================================================================\n\nLlamaIndex offers capabilities to not only build language-based applications but also **multi-modal** applications - combining language and images.\n\nTypes of Multi-modal Use Cases[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#types-of-multi-modal-use-cases \"Permanent link\")\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nThis space is actively being explored right now, but some fascinating use cases are popping up.\n\n### RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation)[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#rag-retrieval-augmented-generation \"Permanent link\")\n\nAll the core RAG concepts: indexing, retrieval, and synthesis, can be extended into the image setting.\n\n*   The input could be text or image.\n*   The stored knowledge base can consist of text or images.\n*   The inputs to response generation can be text or image.\n*   The final response can be text or image.\n\nCheck out our guides below:\n\n*   [GPT-4V Multi Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/gpt4v_multi_modal_retrieval/)\n*   [Multi-modal retrieval with CLIP](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/multi_modal_retrieval/)\n*   [Image to Image Retrieval](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/image_to_image_retrieval/)\n*   [Structured Image Retrieval](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/structured_image_retrieval/)\n*   [Chroma Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/ChromaMultiModalDemo/)\n*   [Gemini Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/gemini/)\n*   [Ollama Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/ollama_cookbook/)\n\n### Structured Outputs[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#structured-outputs \"Permanent link\")\n\nYou can generate a `structured` output with the new OpenAI GPT4V via LlamaIndex. The user just needs to specify a Pydantic object to define the structure of the output.\n\nCheck out the guide below:\n\n*   [Multi-Modal Pydantic Program](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/multi_modal_pydantic/)\n\n### Retrieval-Augmented Image Captioning[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#retrieval-augmented-image-captioning \"Permanent link\")\n\nOftentimes understanding an image requires looking up information from a knowledge base. A flow here is retrieval-augmented image captioning - first caption the image with a multi-modal model, then refine the caption by retrieving it from a text corpus.\n\nCheck out our guides below:\n\n*   [Llava + Testla 10Q](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/llava_multi_modal_tesla_10q/)\n\n### Agents[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#agents \"Permanent link\")\n\nHere are some initial works demonstrating agentic capabilities with GPT-4V.\n\n*   [Multi-Modal Agents](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/mm_agent/)\n*   [GPT-4V Experiments](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/gpt4v_experiments_cot/)\n\nEvaluations and Comparisons[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#evaluations-and-comparisons \"Permanent link\")\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nThese sections show comparisons between different multi-modal models for different use cases.\n\n### LLaVa-13, Fuyu-8B, and MiniGPT-4 Multi-Modal LLM Models Comparison for Image Reasoning[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#llava-13-fuyu-8b-and-minigpt-4-multi-modal-llm-models-comparison-for-image-reasoning \"Permanent link\")\n\nThese notebooks show how to use different Multi-Modal LLM models for image understanding/reasoning. The various model inferences are supported by Replicate or OpenAI GPT4-V API. We compared several popular Multi-Modal LLMs:\n\n*   GPT4-V (OpenAI API)\n*   LLava-13B (Replicate)\n*   Fuyu-8B (Replicate)\n*   MiniGPT-4 (Replicate)\n*   CogVLM (Replicate)\n\nCheck out our guides below:\n\n*   [Replicate Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/replicate_multi_modal/)\n*   [GPT4-V](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/openai_multi_modal/)\n\n### Simple Evaluation of Multi-Modal RAG[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#simple-evaluation-of-multi-modal-rag \"Permanent link\")\n\nIn this notebook guide, we'll demonstrate how to evaluate a Multi-Modal RAG system. As in the text-only case, we will consider the evaluation of Retrievers and Generators separately. As we alluded to in our blog on the topic of Evaluating Multi-Modal RAGs, our approach here involves the application of adapted versions of the usual techniques for evaluating both Retriever and Generator (used for the text-only case). These adapted versions are part of the llama-index library (i.e., evaluation module), and this notebook will walk you through how you can apply them to your evaluation use cases.\n\n*   [Multi-Modal RAG Evaluation](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/evaluation/multi_modal/multi_modal_rag_evaluation/)\n\nModel Guides[#](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/multimodal/#model-guides \"Permanent link\")\n---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nHere are notebook guides showing you how to interact with different multimodal model providers.\n\n*   [OpenAI Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/openai_multi_modal/)\n*   [Replicate Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/replicate_multi_modal/)\n*   [Ollama Multi-Modal](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/examples/multi_modal/ollama_cookbook/)\n\nBack to top\n\n[Previous Agents](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/agents/)[Next Fine-Tuning](https://docs.llamaindex.ai/en/stable/use_cases/fine_tuning/)\n\n![Image 6](https://static.scarf.sh/a.png?x-pxid=2b5669c2-eb91-4d0a-81d6-dc7238350598)",
```json
  "usage": {
    "tokens": 50343
  }
}
```
